 phir haathon main isaki gandh bhi rah jaati he jo der tak pareshaan karti he
 If you want to make this task easier then we have a solution for you
 is upaay se mahaj paanch minute menaap apni tokari main rakhe lahasun ko saaf kar sakati hai:trick
 1
 ek katori main pani bhar len or lahasun kii kaliyon ko usamen dubo den
 After one hour, place these buds on the slab and press it lightly
 lahusun kaa chhilka khud ba khud saaf ho jayega
 Trick
 2
 With the help of a knife, cut the top of the garlic
 isse lahasun kaa chhilka jaldi se saaf ho jayega
 If garlic is to be chopped, chop it in advance
 kaatane ke baad lahasun kaa chhilka aasaani se utar jaataa he
 Trick
 3
 Put all the garlic buds in the microwave for 30 seconds
 jab aap ise microwave se nikaalengi to iskaa chhilka roast ho chukaa hoga or bahut aasaani se utar jayega
 Trick
 4
 If you do not have a microwave, you can also heat garlic peels on the pan or pan
 iske baad inkaa chhilka aaraam se utar jayega
 Trick
 5
 Put garlic buds in a box and shake it vigorously for one or two minutes

 — ANI (@ani_news)july 18, 2017 After the robbery in Gurgaon, adjoining the capital Delhi, a case of rape has come to light
 chaar nakaabposh badmaashon ne is vaardaat ko anjaam diya he
 The miscreants first robbed the house and then raped the woman
 maamla sector 10 thane main darj kiya gaya he
 However, so far no one has been arrested in this case
 fesasbook ne android or ios par massenger ap ke liye ek nayaa apadet jari kiya he
 After this update, users will be able to make group audio calling
 agle 24 se 48 ghante main yah nayaa apadet aapke smartphone main bhi dastak de saktaa he
 After updating, you will see the phone icon in Messenger
 us par tap karke aap members ko aid kar sakate hai
 Those you add to the group call will get a message
 agar kisi ne kol except nahinkia to kol ke bichamen bhi jud sakate hai
 Also during the call you can see who is connected to it
 jo log pehali baar main kol main nahin jud paae honge, unhen dobaaraa request bhej sakate hai
 According to Facebook, up to 50 people can interact at once
 yani 50 se zyada members nahin jode ja sakate
 Earlier the company had stated its limit to 12, later it has been increased to 50
 gauratlab he ki fasebuk ne 2013 main voip (wais ower internet protocol) yani audio colling kii shuruyaat kii thi, tab sirf ek baar main ek yujar se hi baat kii ja sakati thi
 The Congress Party of India has challenged the jurisdiction of an American court to hear the 1984 Sikh riots
 america main ek sikh sanghathan kii yachika par yah sunwaayee ho rahi he
 During a hearing in a US federal court on Wednesday, Judge Robert Sweet said Congress had challenged the court's right to hear the case and had not produced any evidence to defend the charges against it
 sikh for justise (esaje) ne pichley varsh march main yachika daayar kii thi
 According to SFJ, the Congress advocates said that the court summons at the party headquarters in New Delhi has not been received
 sanghathan ne aarope lagaaya tha ki tatkaaleen pradhanmantri indira gandhi kii hatya ke baad puure desh main sikhon ke khilaaf hue niojit dangon main congress kii bhoomika thi
 On December 21, the High Court rejected Sajjan Kumar's request to extend the surrender period to January 30 in the court
 sajjan kumaar ne yah avadhi badhaane kaa anurodh karte huye kaha tha ki unhen apane bacchon or sampatti se sambandhit kuch paariwarik masale nipataane hai or court main is faisle ko chunauti dene ke liye bhi samay kii aavashyaktaa he
 The case of anti-sikh riots involving Sajjan Kumar is related to the killing of five Sikhs and the burning of a gurdwara on November 1-2, 1984 in Raj Nagar part-i of Palam Colony in southwest Delhi
 danga peediton kaa pratinidhitiv kar rahe varisht adhivaktaa ech es phulka napehle hi sheersh adaalat main ek arji daayar kar rakhi he taaki sajjan kumaar ke paksh main ekatarfa koi aadesh nahin sunaaya ja sake
 The High Court quashed the lower court's 2010 judgment acquitting Sajjan Kumar in the case
 maamle main anya doshiyon main congress ke purv parshad balavaan khokhar, nausena ke sevanivrutt adhikari captain bhaagamal, girdhaari laal or purv vidhayak mahendar yadav or kishan khokhar shaamil hai

 isliye palaayan ko lekar pareshaan mat hoiye
 We have our own country and will live somewhere, but understand the conditions of wages and living conditions
 use badalane kii baat kijiye
 Take these leaders who shared the dreams of stopping the migration in Bihar and Uttar Pradesh and take them to the labor settlements here and ask that say this will change the situation
 dukh he ki ye halaat nahin badalte
 a similar report was reported from Kapashera in Delhi in 2010
 2015 main gudgaanv se thik aisi hi report kii
 Reported the same in 2012 from a labor colony in Surat
 halaat bilkul nahin badale hai
 In any state and in any government
 har cameraa ab do se dhai hajaar kaa he
 Let two to three laborers stay in one room
 aamtaur par chaar-paanch mazdoor dhai hajaar kaa kiraaya saajha kar lete hai, lekin makaan maalikon ne aise niyam banaae hai ki ek kamare main do yaa teen se zyada mazdoor nahin rah sakate 
 They do so because the land is limited
 kamaron kii sankhya simit he
 To be sure, the number of laborers working is also limited
 agar ek kamare main das rahenge to baaki kamaron kaa kya hoga
 Therefore only two remain
 dhai hajaar kaa kiraaya unki chah hajaar kii kamai ko nigal jaataa he
 These rooms have another condition
 har campus main yaa har makaan maalik kii kiraane kii ek dukaan he
 The landlord decides from which shop the tenant will buy the goods
 vahaan har saamaan kaa bhav bazaar dar se zyaada hota he
 Like i was told by a boy that ten kilos of flour comes in two and a half hundred, but the landlord sells it at his shop for two hundred and ninety
 chalis rupee zyada
 The landlord is aware that customers from other campuses will not visit his shop, as every campus tenant has to buy from his owner's shop
 makaan maalik kam graahakon kii sankhya kii bharpai daam badha kar letaa he
 If you do not buy the goods from the landlord's shop, he will remove it from the room
 mazdooron ne bataaya ki unke bag check kiye jate hai
 The landlord also keeps track of how many days the tenant buys the goods
 agar koi das din baad aataa letaa he or khatm hone par duusari jagah se kam keemat par aataa le aae to makaan maalik ko pataa chal jaataa he ki is baar aataa to karidaa nahin to kha kya rahaa hoga
 The owner checks the room and removes it if caught
 nikaale jane par agar duusare campus main gaye bhi to vahaan bhi inhen sharton par rahanaa hoga
 Landlords have learned these terms of eviction from the company owners
 jaise wo kam mehtaanaa dekar zyaada mazaduri karaate hai or bolne par naukari se nikaal dete hai
 In the same way, the landlord loots the earnings in his tenant's pocket by all means
 andaman ke cellular jail se bhaagane par samandar miltaa tha
 Some freedom fighters also escaped from prison, but drowned in the sea a little further away
 mar gaye
 This is the condition of these workers of Gurgaon
 sarkaar bhale hi tamaam aankadon se bataati rahe ki mahangaai kam ho gai he, magar in lakhon beawaz mazaduron ko adhik daam main khareednaa padataa he
 Even after this oppression, the landlord does not even clean the rooms
 sau kamare par paanch shauchalay hai
 Their doors are broken
 peshaab kii durgandh se puraa campus mahaktaa milegaa
 Sick people will be seen in any room
 sochiye agar aapke saath aisi bandish ho ki usee dukaan se or bade hue daam se saamaan khareednaa hoga to kya haalat hogi
 The newspaper does not come in the room of these workers
 zyaadaatar ke kamare main tivi nahin he
 TV is installed in the shops, where a crowd of ten and twenty workers are standing and eradicating their fatigue with the songs of Govinda
 iskaa matlab yah nahin ki akhabaaron or tivi main inhen kii khabaren aati hai, jiske liye inhen channel dekhnaa chahie, balki samajhadaari kaa kaam yahi kiya he ki akhbaar or channel nahin liye hai, varanaa maheene ke do sau teen sau rupee us chah hazaar kii kamai se or lutaa jate
 The comments sab kaam milane kii baaten karte hai
 As soon as the election comes, the leader says that the migration will stop
 bihar, upi main udyog khulene ke vaade kiye jate hai
 Try visiting Gurgaon and its adjoining Delhi villages
 kin sharton par logon ko kaam mil rahaa he
 Have been working on the same salary for ten years
 bihar main bhi to yahi udyog jaaenge
 They can be used anywhere, but their pattern is the same
 vahaan bhi ye cellular jail banaaenge
 They will work for fifteen hours with less salary and take away the freedom to buy food
 isliye palaayan ko lekar pareshaan mat hoiye
 We have our own country and will live somewhere, but understand the conditions of wages and living conditions
 use badalane kii baat kijiye

 a similar report was reported from Kapashera in Delhi in 2010
 2015 main gudgaanv se thik aisi hi report kii
 Reported the same in 2012 from a labor colony in Surat
 halaat bilkul nahin badale hai
 In any state and in any government
 in kamaron kii ek or shart he
 Every campus or every homeowner has a grocery store
 makaan maalik tay karata he ki kiraayedaar kis dukaan se saamaan khridega
 Every item there is priced higher than the market rate
 jaise mujhe ek ladke ne bataaya ki das kilo aataa dhai sau main aata he, lekin makaan maalik apni dukaan par do sau nabbe main bechata he
 Forty rupees more
 makaan maalik ko pataa he ki uski dukaan par duusare campus ke graahak nahin aaenge, kyonki har campus ke kiraayedaar ko apane maalik kii dukaan se hi kareednaa padataa he
 The landlord compensates for the reduced number of customers by increasing the price
 agar aap makaan maalik kii dukaan se saamaan nahin kharidenge to vah kamare se nikaal degaa
 The workers reported that their bags are checked
 makaan maalik iskaa bhi hisaab rakhata he ki kitne dinon main koun kiraayedaar saamaan kharidta he
 If someone takes the flour after ten days and when it is finished, bring the flour at a lower price than the other place, then the landlord comes to know that this time, if he did not buy the flour or not, what would have happened
 maalik kamare kii checking kar daalata he or pakade jane par nikaal detaa he
 If you go to other campuses on removal, then you will have to live there on the same conditions
 makaan maalikon ne nikaale jane kii ye sharten company waalon se sikhi he
 Like they pay less wages and get more wages and get fired from speaking jobs
 vaise hi makaan maalik apane kiraayedaar kii jeb main ai kamai ko har tarah se lutata he
 The sea was found when Andaman escaped from the Cellular Jail
 kuch swatantraaa senaanee jail se bhaage bhi, lekin samandar main thodi dur tair kar dub gaye
 died
 thik yahi haalat gudgaanv ke in mazdooron kii he
 Even though the government keeps telling from all the figures that inflation has come down, but these millions of unemployed laborers have to buy more
 is julm ke baad bhi makaan maalik kamaron kii safai tak nahin karaata
 There are five toilets on a hundred rooms
 unke darvaaze tak toote hai
 The entire campus will get added importance due to the smell of urine
 kisi bhi kamare main jhaankiye biimaar log milenge
 Think if there is such a restriction with you that you will have to buy goods from the same shop and at a higher price, what will be the situation
 in mazaduron ke kamare main akhbaar nahin aata he
 Most rooms do not have tvs
 dukaanon main tivi laga he, jahaan das bees mazaduron kii bheed khadi hokar govinda ke gane se apni thakaan mitaa rahi hoti he
 This does not mean that these are the news reports in newspapers and TV, for which they should watch the channel, but have done the work of understanding that newspapers and channels have not been taken, otherwise two hundred three hundred rupees of the month earned that six thousand
 Used to rob
 tippaniyan Everyone talks about getting work
 chunaav aate hi netaa bolta he ki palaayan band ho jayega
 Promises to open industries are made in Bihar, UP
 gudgaanv or usase sate dilli ke gaanvon main jaakar dekh lijie
 Under what conditions are people getting work
 das-das saal se ek hi selary par kaam kar rahe hai
 The same industries will also go to Bihar
 ye kahin bhi lagen, lekin inkaa pattern to ek hi he
 They will also build cellular jails there
 kam tankhwaah dekar pandrah ghante kaam karaayenge or khaanaa kareedne tak kii azaadi chin lenge
 So don't worry about migration
 apana hi desh he kahin rah lenge, lekin mazaduri or rahane ke jo halaat hai, use samajhiye
 Talk about changing it
 bihar or uttar pradesh main palaayan band karaane ke sapane baantne vaale in netaaon ko yahaan kii mazdoor bastiyon main le jaakar puuchhiye ki bolo ye halaat badal doge
 Sadly, this situation does not change
